Foreword  
                   President of the World Peace and Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)  
Good and Evil, Rise and Fall  
Matthew 5:43-48  
<Prayer (I)> Today is June 22, 1969, a Sabbath day. On this day, your children have gathered in the sanctuary from all directions, and we earnestly wish and hope for your infinite compassion and mercy to be bestowed upon us.  
We reflect once again on how much we have raised your name and how much joy we have brought you while fighting against the affairs of the world for a week. We realize that we must once again critique and analyze ourselves as individuals in light of this past time, focusing on the present reality. Father, we earnestly wish and hope for this.  
We know that many of your children have fallen while seeking the true path throughout the long course of history and fighting for the true cause. However, we also recognize the sad fact that no one has lived on this earth as a true person with true victory in the genuine sense.  
History has been connected around such a focal point, and at this present moment, we must also connect around that same focal point, clearly stating that we are the ones who must determine the final destiny. We must establish ourselves centered on you, Father, and centered on your will, and this must be a time to reaffirm that commitment.  
June 22, 1969 (Sun), at the former headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).  
* This message is also published in <Seonghwa> No. 90 (August 1969 issue).  

8   Good and Evil, Rise and Fall  
When comparing my past self with my present self, if I cannot bring about a meaningful difference in goodness, our future path will undoubtedly be a bleak one. Furthermore, as our enemies mock and deceive us, we will inevitably encounter a fate akin to a ship caught in a storm. If that happens, we must clearly understand that this will be our fate, and at this moment, allow us to reaffirm ourselves so that we can establish a connection with you, Father.  
Father, please help us to realize that the root of sin remains in our hearts and bodies, which we cannot overcome by our own strength. Help us to recognize that we have come this far through various experiences from the past until now and to feel deeply that we need a stimulating driving force to revolutionize our present selves.  
Unless we establish ourselves anew, removing our current selves to create a new self for tomorrow, we will not be able to remain as anything worthy in the path of good will and good history. We earnestly wish and hope for this realization.  
Please do not let us become pitiful people whose lives flow away with the passing waves, and help us to clearly understand that the purpose of goodness remains for us to swim against those waves.  
Through the course of history, we know that the will of heaven does not disappear with history but rather seeks to manage and elevate history. We understand that it is only in such a path that God has worked alongside us. We also recognize that we are those who have already practiced this at one time. However, at this moment, we earnestly wish and hope to reflect on where we stand and to be in a position to receive your guidance, Father.  
Help us to fully understand that you are always with goodness and never participate in absolute evil. You came forth with a purpose to be united with goodness, to work with goodness, and to fulfill a purpose with goodness. Therefore, even if our bodies are removed, we must be those whose hearts are eternally united with goodness.  
Thus, may our hearts direct and command our bodies to submit and be governed, so that we can become the self that aligns with your eternal will, Father. We earnestly wish and hope for this. May this time be one where we can reaffirm our desire to become such a self, to gather ourselves again, and to reaffirm our resolution to become such a self.  
Father! Since the beginning of this June, we have entered a special period. During this time, each of us must prepare a true heart as sons and daughters before you, who have borne the grief of 6,000 years. We also know that we must establish a foundation for complete victory based on the global ideals you desire in our families. Therefore, Father, please be with us based on the sincerity of each individual and family.  
Centered on this 120-day period, we wish to convey all our stories before you. They are not for the sake of individual prosperity or the prosperity of this nation and people alone. They are to pave the way for a global destiny and to overcome the great cross of indemnity you have left behind. Thus, may this period be one where we take responsibility and offer special sincerity, allowing us to forget ourselves and prioritize you, Father.  
Father, today your children in Japan have come to this place. They have not come to seek anything of the earth but have come to yearn for a connection that brings them closer to you, feeling the tears and sweat hidden in the footsteps you left behind. Each of us must deeply consider what we can give to these individuals.  
Now, help us to clearly understand that we have entered an era that transcends the individual and the nation to one that can serve the world. In this era, we have turned toward the global stage with you, and we have the opportunity to participate in that great procession. May we be your children who truly understand the preciousness of this public responsibility.  
Father, may this time be one where we, your children from Japan who have come seeking you, and we from Korea can unite to offer worship that truly pleases you.  
We know that those who have been left behind, the members scattered throughout Japan, are longing for this time of worship before you, joining in prayer. Therefore, please be with them in all their prayers and desires, allowing us to leave behind the positive results you wish for.  
Through this gathering today, may your joy be multiplied, and may the connections that please you sprout anew in each of our hearts. For those of your sons and daughters whose faith is still shallow, may this time allow them to lament their own situation and draw closer to your will, Father. We earnestly wish and hope for this.  
In the remaining time, we wish to dedicate our lacking selves within your permission, so please accept us, Father.  
May this time allow us to expose our own shame, to reveal that we cannot present ourselves before you, and to seek your merciful hand. We earnestly wish and hope for this, Father.  
At this time, your children are praying from various places in South Korea and around the world, longing for this headquarters. May your eternal love and grace abundantly manifest in every place where their sincerity reaches, and may we all become dutiful sons and daughters and loyal subjects before you, Father.  
We earnestly request that in the remaining time, only your intended will may operate, and we pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.  
<Prayer (II)> Father, we have come to understand that we must become like little children before you. We know that unless we become like little children and are embraced in your bosom, we cannot establish the relationship of love that allows us to dwell forever within your grace.  
We also understand that we must pass through the age of childhood, the youth stage, the adulthood stage, and the old age stage to return to you, Father. We long for that time when you can embrace us with your true heart of love.  
Father, you desire that we, having grown in this way, stand by your side as your sons and daughters, fulfilling our duties of filial piety and equipping ourselves to confront our enemies in your stead. You wish for us to fulfill our responsibilities to subdue them, bringing forth the glory of victory.  
We know that all this glory belongs to you, so may you receive it. We understand that you wish for us to become the embodiment of the glory of victory. Knowing this, we must be aligned with your complete love from the moment we are born until we die. If we do not find the value in being born on this earth, we will not be able to fulfill the purpose of our lives. We must come to this realization once again at this time.  
Father, we entrust the remaining time to you, so please be with us, and do not let anyone stand on this platform to boast of themselves. Only your long and high holiness may descend here, and may your providence intertwine with the hearts of each individual, allowing us to become one before your grace. We earnestly wish and hope for this, Father.  
We have gathered here not to share any worldly knowledge, nor to discuss any material conditions. We have come together longing for the spring day when we can welcome the foundation of harmony with your love, to enrich our empty inner emotional world, like a dry desert. Each individual’s circumstances and deep stories are with you. May this time allow us to start a relationship that cannot begin or end without you, Father. We earnestly wish and hope for this.  
Just as a child who has lost their parents must have a deep longing for their parents, those who have lost their country must have a sincere heart to fight for their country. We, who have lost the Lord of the universe, must love and yearn for you, the Lord of the universe, more than anyone else.  
We must strive to become ancestors who will faithfully serve the nation and the world you desire, not only for ourselves but also for our families and future generations. Even if we cannot bring about such results, we have gathered here to become your sons and daughters who can sow and plant the inner feelings for it. We earnestly wish and hope that you will come to us, Father.  
We are ashamed that we have nothing to present before you, and we have nothing to cover our shame. Please cover us with your mantle of grace and fill our hunger with your abundant food. For those who have forgotten the hope of tomorrow, please grant them the one purpose of hope, allowing them to gather their strength and make a breakthrough toward that goal. We earnestly wish and hope for this, Father.  
In the depths of our hearts, you have called us millions of times, but we have not responded. You have beckoned us millions of times, but we have not followed. However, we know that your heart of compassion is eternally with the course of human history, so we earnestly wish and hope that you will call us once again, your lacking children.  
Father, at this time, we earnestly wish and hope that everything may begin and end within your will. We also earnestly request that you extend your hand of love to the countless children who are longing for this place, allowing them to join in the same grace. We pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.  
<Words> Today, I will speak briefly on the topic of Good and Evil, Rise and Fall.  
The Standard of Goodness that Remains in the End  
We know well that among the countless humans living on this earth, there is no one who does not wish to be good. Until now, the direction of history has also aimed toward goodness, and we know that educators and believers have fought and made efforts to establish the standard of goodness. Therefore, being born must be for the sake of goodness, living must be for the sake of goodness, and dying must be for the sake of goodness; this is the purpose of life. This is not only the purpose of life but also the purpose of the history that has woven human existence, and we cannot deny this.  
Here, goodness (善) is not a vague concept. It is a goodness with meaning, and it is a centered goodness among goods.  
Some may say, "I live centered on my conscience; how could there be anything unworthy in my life?" However, in claiming to live centered on one’s conscience, one cannot deny the fact that they are the center. No matter how much one believes they are moving in a good direction according to their conscience, if it differs from the direction of goodness that the nation is moving toward, the nation will prosper.
will find that many people live for their own interests, which is indeed a pitiful existence. 

The true purpose of life is not to live for oneself, but to live for the world and humanity. This is the path we must take. 

In conclusion, the ultimate goal of humanity's conscience is to align with the heavenly providence and to become one with God's love. This is the essence of our existence and the direction we must pursue. 

The greatest sages in history are those who clearly teach the direction revealed by God and the heavenly providence, guiding humanity towards the path they should follow. When this understanding manifests in the world, it will naturally unite all people.

From this perspective, it is evident that no nation has successfully imitated such a system. Although many nations have perished, religion has not. As you know from history, the foundation of world culture has been religion. Even when Christianity faced severe persecution in Rome for 400 years, the sovereignty of that nation fell, but Christianity did not perish. Why? Because what aligns with the principles and laws of heaven grows stronger the more it is attacked.

In this context, what is true religion? It teaches goodness that is not merely individual. The concept of goodness we have understood so far varies according to the laws of nations or ethnicities, leading individuals to follow the moral paths dictated by their societies. Therefore, we must consider what the common standard of living is that aligns with the direction of conscience that humanity collectively desires. This is where the issue lies. If someone is born, lives, and dies in such a context, they must go to heaven.

So, what is evil? It is the opposite of good. The standard for determining evil lies in recognizing true goodness and opposing it. Therefore, if one strays from public standards, they will inevitably deviate from the direction of goodness. You can see this for yourselves; in any community, people generally dislike those who try to draw others in for their own benefit. Even minor conditions can lead to hatred. To be hated is to be on the path to destruction. However, those who forget themselves and strive to give to others are universally liked.

Then, what direction do personal, familial, and ethnic fortunes take, and where are they determined? They are not determined by some global event but rather within your own sphere of life. Those who seek to resolve everything centered on themselves will inevitably perish. If you think, "What is yours is mine, and what is mine is mine," you will fail. Therefore, what is yours is not yours but belongs to the nation and the world. The same goes for what is mine.

The rise and fall are determined by the distinction between good and evil. So, where does the line of good and evil begin? It does not begin on the day the Republic of Korea falls. It is drawn in your daily life. The moment you eat and live, the two worlds are divided.

Thus, where does the food you eat come from? Is it produced in a place that aligns with the public standards and the universal laws of heaven, or does it arise from your own desires? This is the critical question.

From this perspective, everything perceived through your senses must change. Those who live with a self-centered perspective will fail. Moreover, such individuals will find no one to help them when they do fail. This is a historical fact and cannot be denied within your sphere of life. No one wishes to fail. If anyone desires failure, let them raise their hand. It is not just the people of Korea; the same goes for the Japanese and all humanity.

So, if all people dislike failure, why does it happen? It is because they do not realize that their way of living and their position do not align with a good place and cannot stand within the providential authority of heaven. When a nation fails, the individual fails too; thus, one must stand for the world even if it means stepping on their own nation. We need individuals who can move toward the great providence of the world and illuminate the path that all humanity must follow.

In this regard, the saying goes that "the righteous will receive blessings from heaven, while the unrighteous will incur heaven's wrath." However, the concept of goodness is vague. What is the center of that goodness? If heaven's wrath is a mere impersonal and abstract concept, then it is unnecessary.

Those who hold a self-centered ideology will fail. The standard of good and evil is not established at the final judgment but is divided based on the current conscience of individuals. Today is like a time of judgment. If an entire nation walks the path aligned with heavenly providence, and that providence flows through individuals, families, ethnicities, and nations, then that nation becomes a chosen people. Historically, the Israelites had the concept of being a chosen people, indicating that they had a connection with heaven.

What is this chosen people? It is a people through whom the greatest providence of heaven flows within their personal living sphere, their family, their ethnicity, and their nation. When the providence can flow through all these aspects, that nation is called a chosen people, existing within the purpose of heaven's providence.

Therefore, those who hold a self-centered ideology will perish. If one harms others for their own desires or brings harm to the nation for their own sake, they will fail. A nation is not to be used by individuals; rather, individuals should be used for the nation. This is the duty of citizens and the direction they must take.

Today, the global trend does not wish to be dominated by communism or democracy. If it is democracy, then it must align with the providence of God, standing in a position that harmonizes with the family, ethnicity, nation, and world to avoid failure. If communism aligns with this, then no matter how much we oppose it, it will not fail. The issue lies here.

Human beings are not originally meant to live solely for themselves. Yet, many people today live only for their own interests. They say, "I work for myself." This is indeed a pitiful existence, akin to an orphan without parents or siblings. One must be able to say, "I live for the sake of humanity." 

No one wishes to live a petty life like a coward. Yet, as history has shown, many people do just that.
It is indeed about living centered on oneself. Such a person will perish along with their own standards. Moreover, their descendants will also suffer miserably. However, a person who does not center themselves and lives from a public standpoint for others, for the nation, for the world, and for heaven and earth will not perish, even if they live in poverty and leave nothing behind. When such a person dies, many people will bow their heads and shed tears, and thus heaven cannot help but bless them.

If Jesus came to this age and prayed, originally, humans could aim for the purpose of goodness and could go to a flourishing world, but because they went astray, they ended up in this position. Therefore, standing in a position that needs to be corrected, we must go with more moral and heavenly content. If we do not, you must understand that this world has nothing but misery and destruction.

Thus, a person like Jesus came to this earth and lived a public life to fulfill his mission as the Messiah and the savior of all humanity. What was his desire? From the day Jesus came to earth, he had to become a global Messiah and save humanity beyond the nation of Israel. In doing so, his wish was to align that world with heavenly fortune and to possess God's essence and God's love. That was Jesus' purpose, and thus he had to start from this perspective.

What was the last prayer Jesus made at the decisive moment in the Garden of Gethsemane while looking at the cross on the path of death? Because Jesus was also human, he had the possibility to say, "Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me." However, Jesus did not pray that way. He stepped on his human nature and said, "Not my will, but yours be done," thus following the great cause of heavenly fortune rather than his own will.

The phrase "Let this cup pass from me" indicates that there is a personal will. Then what does the phrase "Not my will, but yours be done" mean? If Jesus had a family, he would have prayed, "Let it be according to our family's will, but let us be a family that lives for God's family's will."

Also, if Jesus were in a position to lead Christianity worldwide today, what would he pray for? Would he pray for our Methodism, our Presbyterianism, our Catholicism…? Would he make such trivial prayers? If Jesus were alive in this age and prayed for the twelve disciples, would he ask for blessings for them? No. Rather, he would say, "God, the twelve disciples were established for the world, so please place them on the path of purpose for the world." The nation of Israel was prepared for 4,000 years to send one person to bless them, and for that, they must walk the path where they can contribute to the world. Therefore, he would pray that the twelve disciples must walk the path of death even if they have to fight on behalf of the nation.

Only then would he be a global Messiah and savior, wouldn't he? Yet, Jesus could not even make such a prayer. The last prayer he made was, "Not my will, but yours be done." How tragic is that? You must also pray centered on our church's will rather than your own will. Have you ever thought about how much Jesus must have felt wronged for not being able to pray for God's will that aligned with his own will? When God prepared for 4,000 years and established the chosen people of Israel, that nation was supposed to create a state and stand as a central nation in the world. A central nation in the world is not established by subjugating all other nations by force. It must become a central nation in the world by naturally subjugating those nations. It cannot be done with swords and power.

Even looking at the Vietnam War today, the United States has military power dozens of times greater than Vietnam. In terms of the ability to execute any task, Vietnam is only a fraction of that of the United States. With such power, Vietnam cannot protect its own country. The same goes for North Vietnam. The United States spends nearly 100 million dollars a day on war, so they cannot compete in terms of economic, political, or military power. Thus, North Vietnam, knowing this fact, became frustrated and retreated.

What will the world of goodness be achieved by in the future? All humanity must not oppose heavenly fortune and must follow it, standing in the same position as at the beginning, even while dying, prioritizing the world over their own nation, prioritizing God over the world, and striving to find God's love. This must be universalized through families, tribes, nations, and the world, and only when all human conscience aligns in the same direction and stands in a common position will the ideal world begin.

What if you do good? You should not be afraid of putting yourself forward. You should not fear what anyone in heaven and earth says, not even the president of that nation. You must live for the world and for heaven and earth. Even if the world perishes, heaven and earth will remain. Even if the priests of the world perish, heaven and earth will remain. Therefore, you must be strong and courageous for this. This is only possible through religion.

Christianity has woven a history of martyrdom. Then what was the source of strength that allowed them to overcome the path of death smoothly? Anything that does not align with the great way of heavenly principle will perish. Therefore, even if they are criticized for being in a position of destruction, the wealth, power, and national strength mobilized for criticism can be provocative elements that can withdraw the line before God, but they cannot be provocative elements that destroy goodness. This is the belief they held. Christianity has pushed history forward with this strength within the historical age. You must understand that.

During our training session, when a famous person with a doctorate was asked, "What is God's will?" he replied, "That is an easy yet difficult question." If God's will is an easy yet difficult question, it means it will never be fulfilled. That statement indicates that he does not understand God's will well.

What is God's will? Is it to go east or west? We must fulfill God's will centered on religion. However, if we hold onto our own religious views and try to grasp the world, we cannot fulfill the absolute will. When the end comes, numerous religions will inevitably face the fate of destruction because they hold onto the fortune of religion and the fortune of their denomination.

Heavenly fortune is about stepping on the peak of the world's fortune. When the era of heavenly fortune manifests on earth, the denominational and religious authority established until now will collapse, so the religions of that era must be able to ride on heavenly fortune.

The word "unification" is an unpleasant word in front of established churches. The Unification Church feels the same way about established churches. What does the Unification Church want to do? It is a church that seeks unification. What do we want to unify? Is it to unify men and women? No. What good is it to unify men and women trivial matters? 

It is about becoming one with heavenly fortune. Even if the nation is within the fortune of destruction, there must be someone who can hold onto the heavenly fortune that can prevent it. Only then can that nation survive. You must understand this clearly.

That is why the Unification Church has been very active externally until now. If it does not become a religion that purifies society and presents the direction the nation should go, it will perish. It must not be a religion that is digested before the nation or absorbed by the circumstances of the world. It must become a religion that digests these things.

You members of the Unification Church must center your lives around the common standards of living that all humanity's conscience pursues and form the shapes of society, nation, and world. Even if the nations are different and the traditions are different, we must transcend all of that and seek the common point that conscience aims for. This is significant in establishing a point that can transcend the Republic of Korea and be a place where heavenly fortune flows and God can dwell. Once this point is established, individuals, families, societies, nations, and the world with such an environment will unite without any problems.

Where is the issue for us today? Until now, Christianity has been divided into numerous denominations, all claiming to be the best and most righteous. What does the Unification Church have that can unify all those established churches? The Bible says that God causes the sun to shine on both the evil and the good and sends rain on the righteous and the unrighteous. What does this mean? To love those who love you is no different from others, and to love your enemies and pray for those who persecute you is to become a child of God. 

In light of such biblical words, a Unification Church member can become a child of God. Therefore, a Unification Church member must go through such a process. Until now, we have been beaten and persecuted by them, but we have come out praying for them.

Through what does goodness go? The path that can move even the evil is where heavenly fortune flows. Jesus did not subdue Satan through fighting. While walking the path of death, he stood in the position of saving humanity and prayed for the Roman soldiers who were stabbing him with spears to kill him. From this, we can see that he is the Son of God.

Today, the issue we are concerned with is how to liberate the 10 million people of North Korea. To do that, we must not capture them with bullets. In serving heaven and being loyal, we must take the lead. Therefore, all people of the Republic of Korea must unite. We must unite even stronger than the unity that the tyrant Kim Il-sung has forced through threats of violence.

You must become a group that has the dignity to fulfill your responsibilities. Then you will naturally subdue your opponent without fighting. However, if you fight and win, in the end, you are fighting for others. Therefore, what you must understand is that goodness must be centered on individuals, families, tribes, nations, the world, and even heaven and earth.

Today, there are numerous religions on this earth. However, if a religion is one that only seeks blessings for its own household, that religion will perish. If the household perishes, the nation will perish. When the nation perishes, those who have succeeded in that nation will be the first to perish.

There are religions that serve families, tribes, nations, and states. Starting from serving individuals, the broader the scope, the more it becomes a global religion. If a religion has a purpose and ideology that can transcend all humanity, that religion will not perish and will become a historical religion.

To align with the direction of heavenly fortune, how miserable was Jesus' life? He was labeled a traitor to his nation. He was branded as a reactionary who caused chaos in society and was killed. Even when viewed from the perspective of denominations or sovereignty, there was no place for him to stand, and he was a nonbeliever who could not even be accepted in that society. Jesus lived centered on his family as an individual and lived as a member of society as a Jew, but he did not live only for that family nor only for that nation. Israel fell into the fortune of destruction for 2,000 years, but Christianity has not perished and has remained until now. The Jews who drove Jesus out have perished, but Christianity, centered on Jesus who was destined to perish, has developed globally despite being pushed away.

Then what is the reason it did not perish? It is because Jesus placed Christianity on the trajectory where heavenly fortune could accompany it. Christians can live with heavenly fortune as individuals, and families centered on those individuals can do so as well, and denominations can do so as well, which is why Christianity has become a truly global religion today.

These days, when we look at Unification Church members, many people have become more focused on themselves than on the whole. You will perish if that happens. Even when you eat, you should not eat for yourself. You must eat while embracing your nation and the world. Your entire life must be like that. If you live that way and still perish, you can accuse God. You will not perish. If you are in such a position and are hit, the more you are hit, the more your affairs will prosper.

The Unification Church in the Republic of Korea has been beaten until now, but it has not perished. Rather, it has laid a global foundation. In just a few years, the Republic of Korea will have to face issues. The Unification Church will not perish. Rather, it will continue to grow. This is not because I am great. It depends on how one rides on heavenly fortune. The question is how the fortune of individuals aligns with heavenly fortune, how the fortune of families aligns with heavenly fortune, and how the direction of denominations aligns with the direction of heavenly fortune. If this does not align, everything will go wrong. It means it will perish. Even if one is bare and has nothing, how they connect with heavenly fortune based on this standard will determine the outcome. Whether the Unification Church develops globally or not will also be decided here.

So how do we connect with heavenly fortune? Unity is simple. It is centered on good and evil, and good and evil depend on whether one is centered on oneself or on the whole. Therefore, today, we Unification Church members must eliminate self-centeredness. Everyone must agree on this. Thus, we must walk the path of goodness.

In any nation, we must move forward based on that nation. Today, to prevent this nation from perishing, it is an inevitable fact that we must align externally, but we must also align with the direction of internal heavenly principle. If this nation does not understand this, then someone must become a leader and guide it. This is not just the words of Reverend Moon of the Unification Church. If we do not do this, we will perish immediately.

We must become leaders who devote ourselves before God. If there are such leaders, that nation will not perish. If there are people who work day and night for the sake of the people, shedding tears and worrying about the future of this nation and people, and who can become one with heavenly principles, they will not perish. If not, they will perish.

Even if I am buried for the sake of the will, I will not perish. However, for the path we can take, for the foundation where heavenly fortune can dwell, we must not perish. Because we must not perish, even when the feeling of resentment rises, I did not harbor resentment. I could not harbor resentment because I wished for a nation that would not perish. To have a nation that does not perish, one cannot harbor resentment.

You must understand that God has also been guiding this way. This is God's heart to save the world, but if one goes wrong, they will love themselves.
beautiful than anyone else. 

So, what should we do? We must strive to establish a standard that aligns with the heavenly fortune. We need to become individuals who can connect with that heavenly fortune. When public servants work, they should not complain about their low salaries or their difficult living conditions. Instead, they should focus on how to supplement their needs without lowering their standards. If they set their standards low, they will fail. The greater the disparity, the more they will dissolve into their circumstances.

To achieve unity, one must be willing to sacrifice even their life. The providence of restoration has been established through historical efforts, and without a standard that allows one to accompany God and participate in that providence, one will perish. It is crucial to understand how to live one’s life centered on heavenly fortune. You must grasp this well.

Do you want to perish, or do you not want to perish? "I do not want to perish." That is our desire. Therefore, no one wants to perish. Do you say, "I am ugly, so let things be as they will. I don't care what happens to me"? No, that is not the case. An ugly person looks in the mirror and wishes to see themselves as more beautiful than anyone else.

**Youth Era**  
Today, Christians in Korea or around the world call upon Jesus while being complacent in reality. Unification Church members may lag behind in practical aspects, but they must live with conviction.

Additionally, personal change must occur. To establish this era, one must lay the groundwork for victory within the era. Unification Church youth should recognize that certain issues are this way and others are that way. Therefore, we walk this path. This is how it should be.

Success varies according to each person's talent. Some succeed in a year, while others take three years. Some have the talent to succeed in a year, while others must work twice or three times as hard to succeed. Therefore, one must have the conviction to achieve in the remaining ten years what might take thirty years.

For this reason, it is necessary for Unification Church members to solidify their conviction. The teacher has taken risks since the age of 18 and has continued to do so until now. Conviction is the most important issue. Do you understand? To strengthen this, one must sometimes go to high mountains and explore valleys. And it is necessary to go out to evangelize. So, do you want to go evangelizing or not? If you want to go, go; if you don’t, then don’t.

Next, what do young people need? Motivation. Motivation is also necessary. In the past, when I went to the mountains with friends, I would hurry to eat breakfast and say, "Hey! Let's climb the mountain today." And even if I went, I did not want to be last. That’s how the teacher is. Even when I was a student and said I would go to the mountains, I would fully prepare myself, even if I felt sick or had physical issues. If I couldn’t climb, I would pray and go up. "God! I will climb." This is the condition I set for myself. Just following along is not acceptable. One must do their utmost effort and then pray before God. "I am someone who has made this resolution and has this motivation." When one cannot be at the forefront, they must set such conditions. This motivation is essential. If you are going to climb Baegundae, you must have the motivation to carry a wild boar to the top.

Within motivation lies all curiosity. What kind of birds live in the Han River? Oh, it’s summer and hot, but how cool is it at the top of that mountain? Let’s go up and feel the breeze. Wow! What would it be like to see all of Seoul from there? The more such motivations and desires one has, the less it becomes a problem to overcome all the surrounding circumstances.

From a young age, the teacher would look at mountains and wonder, "What is the name of that mountain? What is there on that mountain?" And whenever I thought of something, I would definitely go see it. I also knew everything within a twenty-mile radius of my neighborhood. If there was a pond, I knew where the hole was and what else was there. I would go through the trouble of draining the entire pond to catch a big catfish if I had to.

There was also a pond with only one big carp, and I would set my fishing rod to catch it. However, that carp wouldn’t bite, and I would often catch small fish instead. When I caught a little one, I would say, "You go, you little rascal!" and try to catch that carp again. When I finally caught that carp, the feeling was something that one cannot understand without experiencing it. In fact, the struggle to catch it was forgotten when I finally succeeded.

You all need to have something that can give you that thrill. However, nowadays, when I see young people, they are quick to catch on, saying, "Who wants to go with me?" even when they actually don’t want to go. If a man does that, he will always be a coward. He just follows others around and complains about his situation. It’s unavoidable. Therefore, motivation is the lifeblood of young people.

Therefore, they cannot be theories of this three-dimensional world.

Therefore, a philosophy that can replace this must emerge. In other words, a philosophy based on complete truth must emerge. This must be able to harmonize, connect, and integrate moral principles and religious ideologies.

Otherwise, a unified world cannot be achieved. Until now, although external forms have been established, the truth that can internally manage has not appeared. Characteristics of Unification Thought
The teachings of the Unification Church will become a global issue in the future. As we enter the late 20th century, left and right are fighting and struggling at this moment, it is already too late to shout for any ideology to break through and revive. Such things have been claimed by this era. Everyone has made their own claims, but they have not solved the problems. Therefore, these ideologies are leaning towards the sunset of the last days. If they tilt a little more, the sun will set. When the twilight hour hastens, communism will pass through this world, and democracy will also disappear.
What are the criteria for communism and democracy? They both conclude based on materialism. Democracy refers to a free economic system, while communism refers to a system of material sharing. Ultimately, they both arrive at conclusions centered around material. Humans are not centered around material. Ideologies do not stem from any material. However, because there has not yet been a standard that concludes beyond material, we must surely walk the second path. Such tasks remain. This is where the unification thought emerges.

This must not disregard historical significance. It must also pursue future potential. In other words, it must seek consistency across the past, present, and future. Because there was a mission to make a new start on the foundation that Heaven had prepared, the teacher went to North Korea. I want to tell you one thing: Mr. Heo Ho-bin walked that path with all her devotion throughout her life. If you look at the history behind that, she walked a path that you cannot imagine. Even under the oppression of the communists, who treated religious people like enemies, she maintained her faith despite extreme torture. The details of the torture are beyond words. I heard that during the hot summer, they were beaten so much that their clothes were full of holes. They fainted dozens of times, and her brother died from the torture. More than 40 of the leaders were also imprisoned and tortured in miserable conditions. The teacher was also treated the same way and imprisoned. The person the teacher still cannot forget is a man named Hong, who was in charge of the investigation at that time, and Park Chan-jeong, who was responsible for the entire situation. <Words> In our daily lives, when what I have is insufficient, every moment of the day can bring joy or sorrow depending on the movement of my heart. Humans are born and die in such a life. We often say, "Today I am lucky," or "Today I am unlucky." Experiencing such emotions in our lives is not a coincidence; it is connected to a person's qualities and the overall circumstances of their life as they pursue a certain purpose.

The purpose of the individual must align with the purpose of the whole.
There is nothing in existence on this earth that is unnecessary. It means that nothing exists without a purpose. Every being exists with a specific purpose, and it goes through a process, or a temporal distance, until that purpose is achieved. This period can be a day, a year, three years, or even a lifetime. For instance, looking at a nation, a nation runs toward its singular purpose of goodness over centuries and millennia. In this way, all beings are running toward the expectation of the purpose for which they exist.

When we look at humans, there are stages of boyhood, youth, adulthood, and old age. The boyhood stage is different from the youth stage, the youth stage is different from the adulthood stage, and the adulthood stage is different from the old age stage. Each of these stages has its own responsibilities and missions. Therefore, if one fails to fulfill their mission in boyhood, they cannot embrace youth vigorously; if they fail to fulfill their mission in youth, they cannot embrace adulthood vigorously. Likewise, if they fail to fulfill their mission in adulthood, they cannot embrace old age vigorously.

In this way, whether a person fulfills the mission given to them in each stage of their life will determine whether they take responsibility for their descendants and, in other words, whether they can establish the purpose standards that are to come.

The same is true for the history of the Republic of Korea. The Republic of Korea is moving toward a singular purpose. This purpose is not limited to the Republic of Korea alone; it carries a shared responsibility to cooperate with all nations around the world. Thus, while fulfilling the purpose of the Republic of Korea, it must also align with the purpose of the world.

In this regard, the history of restoration is similar. Within the history of restoration, there are stages of boyhood, youth, adulthood, and old age. It is structured in such stages. Also, when looking at a day, there is morning, noon, evening, and night. Therefore, morning must be prepared for morning, noon for noon, evening for evening, and night for night, and there are responsibilities assigned within those time frames that we cannot deny.

Restoring this fallen earth is no different. According to our principles, restoration also goes through the stages of rebirth, growth, and perfection. Just as the entire realm of restoration is divided into these stages, we must recognize that there are such principles in our life journey today. Therefore, as you engage in faith within the Unification Church, you must clearly understand whether you are in the stage of rebirth, growth, or perfection. Without understanding this position, you cannot complete the subjective mission that you must fulfill as you prepare for your purpose and move toward it.

Each of you has different qualities, and therefore, each has different purposes in life. The individual purpose varies according to the character of the individual. Thus, while individuals have their own purposes, these individual purposes must connect to the purpose of the whole. For this reason, the standard that education and morality have aimed for until now has been to live for the purpose of the whole rather than for the individual purpose. Therefore, standing in a position where one must live for the whole rather than for the individual, a person must live for the public good rather than for personal gain.

The public good represents the whole rather than the individual. The public issue is established from the perspective of the whole. Ultimately, what an individual does is for themselves. From this perspective, an individual cannot exist alone; they must stand within the environment where the whole lives. To do this, the individual must align vertically with the whole, centering on the whole, and become a standard before the whole. When aligning with heavenly fortune and direction, one exists eternally.
People say, "You must live rightly," or "You must live straight." So what does it mean to live rightly? The standard for living rightly is not centered on oneself. When we look at a tree on a mountain and say, "That tree is straight," it is only from my perspective that it appears straight. However, the true meaning is that if it grows at a 90-degree angle from the ground and environment, then that tree can be considered straight.

Similarly, the standard by which we can judge right and wrong is not centered on ourselves. The public standard, the natural standard, is centered on the principle or the heavenly way. Therefore, we must align ourselves with that public standard to be right. Although we may not clearly understand this, we often speak of what is right or wrong based on such principles. In this regard, we must move toward the purpose of the whole rather than our individual purposes. Thus, before the purpose of the whole, the individual purpose must always align with it.

For this reason, those who walk through life with their innate purpose parallel to the direction of heaven and earth will surely return eternally with heavenly fortune. However, if there is a collision, the fortune of the individual will be crushed by heavenly fortune.
