Until now, even when you have eaten, you have eaten alone. You have lived from that perspective until now. What does it mean to gain salvation through serving in the Unification Church? It means not eating alone but eating together with parents. Isn’t that wonderful? Even when going out, it is not going alone but going with parents.

You must understand how great and serious the concept of living with heaven and earth is. When you truly realize this, there will be no one who does not surrender or submit to it. Those who have that spirit and undoubtedly experience and feel it will not succumb to anything. Even if they were to yield outside of the principles, they will inevitably return to those principles, so ultimately, it is not yielding. Even if they yield, the standards of the principles are different.

That is why the Unification Church urges you to completely surrender and experience this. Then, there will be no reason to be conquered by the world, and salvation will be obtained through serving. Therefore, the Unification Church claims that salvation is obtained through the life of serving. Do you understand? A religion with such conviction can surpass anywhere in the world. From this perspective, you must understand how great the ideology of our Unification Church is today. What else can humanity be thankful for and hope for if not this? This has been the wish of our ancestors until now. It has been the wish of countless men and the wish of countless women. Therefore, if such men and women were to unite on this earth and form a family, they would have become a core existence that heaven and earth could recognize. That is the time when such men and women can open the door to a new world along with heavenly emotion.
The time has come for the failing paradise to take off. Only then will the end of heaven and earth come from there, and a settlement point of purpose and hope that humanity has longed for will emerge. 
When that time comes, the era of claiming to be the best will pass. It will not be a time where one can say, "I am the best." From that point on, it will be a world of coexistence. In other words, it will be a world of co-prosperity, co-ownership, and co-justice. This is why the Unification Church advocates coexistence, co-prosperity, and co-justice. That world cannot be achieved alone. Do you understand? The world of co-prosperity, co-ownership, and co-justice is the ideal heavenly world that humanity has long desired. That world is absolutely unattainable alone.

Coexistence, co-prosperity, and co-justice
Therefore, that world is not one where one exists alone. If I exist, there must be a counterpart, and there must also be a family. This is not just an idea; it must be applied in real life. The world that can be expressed in the stage of life is precisely the world of heaven. Is that not so? 
Everyone, do the left eye and right eye coordinate well? This is co-prosperity. Everyone lives for one purpose. Everything is like this. There are two nostrils, but if one nostril is blocked, is that good or bad? Similarly, if one ear is blocked, is that good or bad? Is it good to be disabled? Try cutting off a leg or an arm. It would feel unpleasant. Therefore, all beings that have a relative relationship prove heaven and earth by themselves. In other words, humans are proving themselves. The heart knows this. The saying that the heart of humanity is the heart of heaven is related to this.

Parental love, spousal love, sibling love—these do not exist in Western thought. Thus, in terms of emotional aspects, Eastern thought is one step higher than Western thought. And from that foundation, the Unification Church advocates coexistence, co-prosperity, and co-justice. Therefore, without departing from this perspective, one cannot exist. One cannot achieve victory alone. This is something you all know well.

Then, what does it mean when I tell you to work for the church? It is to grow bigger. Can you claim to be the leader in your family? Working for the church is for me to grow bigger, working for the nation is for me to grow bigger, working for the world is for me to grow bigger, and working for heaven and earth is also for me to grow bigger. How much bigger? To be the biggest. Here, being big does not refer to volume but to possessing the utmost harmony and maturity both inside and out. You must become people who want to live together with all people on a global level centered around the Unification Church. Only then can you become the sons and daughters of God who created heaven and earth. You must all understand that my path to walk in this perspective remains.

The starting point of this path has been established by the Unification Church. Now that we have started, you must become those who stay at the destination. Therefore, evangelize for the nation. Or become missionaries for the world. Next, for heaven and earth, fight against the Communist Party. From this perspective, I hope you recognize your own value well and live in the place that God desires today.

<Prayer> Father, until now, we have thought that our one life is a pitiful existence. However, now let us clearly understand that our one life has been shaped along with history. 
Let us discover here that due to our own sorrow, we are unable to express our hearts and that we are beings who cannot get angry. 
Father, how much have we respected our own selves that are connected in this way? We have realized that the shining history is not in the relative world, but behind the history of our own being. We have understood that the glory of victory is not in some world of heaven but that the place where the gift of victory can remain along with history depends on our own being. Therefore, Father, no matter how vast the world may be, if I cannot determine the place where I can stay, that world becomes extremely narrow, and although my own being is extremely small, if I have determined the internal foundation that can bend the entire world, may I be able to discover that my being is one that the whole world can resemble and more. Thus, Jesus said, "What good is it for someone to gain the whole world, yet forfeit their soul?" and Buddha proclaimed the value of "I alone am honored in heaven and on earth." Let us realize that all of this cannot exist apart from our own being.

Father, please look after your children gathered here. Even if their appearances are different, we understand that the path we must walk is the same. Even if their hearts are torn apart, we must have a standard that can gather them into one heart. We have also understood that the facts of actions are determined from here. Therefore, when a spiritual standard that can determine this place appears, we will surely understand that a new heaven will be established from here and that the wheels of new history will begin to turn.

In this regard, we have come to understand how great the mission of the Unification Church is. Therefore, we must laugh at the past history that ended with mere recognition and elevate the value of recognition along with heaven and earth to a thousandfold and ten thousandfold. Therefore, we must realize that to stand in a position where we can proudly say, "I am the one who has what all people in the world desire and idealize in the world of heart," we must pass through the door of unity.

When we think that such solemn and valuable content can become the source of joy that shines along with the long history of ten thousand years or with the existence of the entire universe, we must truly be grateful for having come to know this place. Therefore, may this place become one where we can fulfill our duties of loyalty and responsibility before the Father, beyond the labor of seeking until now.

Father! Now, when we come to know that the heart and the standard of praise that can sing of the joy and happiness you desire are here, may we recognize that this place is where we can pour out our entire body and mind. The children of unity must deeply feel that after knowing this path, they must forget all their environments and follow this path centered on the church. 
Father, to walk this path, our bodies must follow our hearts. This is not some kind of magic or a new harmony, but we realize that it is a natural law that moves according to the principles of heaven. Therefore, we earnestly hope and desire that we may bring about results that can absolutely achieve victory according to the principle of compliance.

The path we walk is not for anyone else. It is a path for ourselves, and at the same time, it is a path for the world and the nation. Let us understand that we do not live for some individual, but we live for the world. When I was born, I was not born just for Kim so-and-so. Let me be able to boast that I was born to walk this path and to know that it is the heavenly principle of my life. May I become a being who can clarify this issue and solve it, and find a core reality that can further enhance that value, which is the purpose of being a member of the Unification Church.

Father, we have come to realize that walking this path is more urgent than anything else in the world. When we ask who we have gathered for, we have not gathered for the teacher of the Unification Church, nor for anything of the Unification Church. We seek the Unification Church for ourselves, and we believe and follow it because there is a nation and a world that the Unification Church desires, and this path is the closest path to that. Therefore, Father, may the unchanging heart that desires to move toward the nation through the Unification Church, toward the world through the Unification Church, and toward heaven through the Unification Church not be broken, and may that heart flow out abundantly.

May the heartbeat of the arteries flowing from the heart and the heartbeat resonating through the heart of heaven allow us to fulfill the role of veins that move and circulate our living emotions. Thus, may the pulse of that vein shine brightly in history and become the companion of all people in life. May we come to understand that this is what you, Father, are asking us even at this moment.

Father, we must praise the precious "me" for eternity. For that "me" that must be established, we must fight even if it means shedding the blood of all fallen descendants. Today's struggle is to illuminate tomorrow's "me," and with that brightness, we hope to nurture the relationships of heaven and earth. May we become heavenly warriors who can respect even a single moment of today. I earnestly ask you, loving Father.

Now, where is our heart flowing? Where is our body resting? May we not remain in the place of the heart of the past, and may we not become beings who hide in a self that can perish in the past and remain in a place where we can be punished. 
May we be able to equip our bodies and hearts to sprout in the hearts of humanity on earth, carrying the heart of the Father, kneeling before the Father, pledging our loyalty, and envisioning that "me" who can become a light in ten thousand affairs, and may we be able to embody the appearance of the princes and princesses of the Father. May the place where the passion of admiration for the Father can sprout, or the place where the passion of longing can shine, become our own being.

We must rally for a shining tomorrow. We must rally for a shining tomorrow's "me." We must rally for a shining new heaven. To do this, we must become vessels suitable for that. We must equip ourselves inside and out to shine. We must also sleep peacefully before the relationships of heaven and earth, awaken peacefully, and become the sons and daughters of the Father, and we must become true children who can genuinely call upon the Father. Therefore, I earnestly ask you, loving Father, that all your sons and daughters may be able to sing of their daily lives in that love and to praise the daily affairs in that story.

May the remaining time be glorious, and may this place become a true place for praising me. I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 

Let us live in our house
<Summary of the Message> The house we live in today is not our true home. 
If there is a house where God resides, everything will be connected around that house. 
The foundation of happiness is the family. 
People tend to think that happiness starts from within themselves. So, who is in our house? Parents, siblings, relatives, our village—when all these conditions are met, a person is happy. 
Happiness cannot be felt by one person alone. It must be something that brings joy to my parents, siblings, and spouse together. 
The house is where joy can be felt relatively or subjectively. A person who does not have this is like an orphan. We call someone who does not have a house to live in an orphan. 
We absolutely need our house, not someone else's house. Without leaving the house, which is the foundation of complete happiness, neither the nation nor the world, nor any purpose can be established. 
September 7, 1969 (Sunday) early morning, at the former headquarters church. 
* This message was recorded by Chairman Yoo Kwang-ryeol of the Historical Compilation Committee in a notebook during Sunday morning service and has been organized for publication.

We must become parents, spouses, and siblings centered on the house that God desires. 
The factors of happiness and resentment spread out from the house to the nation and the world. 
The starting point and the conclusion that God desires is the house. However, we have not been able to establish the house that God envisions. Rather, the closer we get to the purpose, the closer we are to destruction and unhappiness in the house we live in today. 
No one knew that the house, the foundation of the highest happiness, would become a foundation of despair and disbelief. Heaven has been working until now to restore this. Such familial unhappiness began from the time of Adam and Cain. 
From here, we must establish the eternal ideal house. This is the house called the Unification Church today. The group that walks the path that others say is not the way to establish the house that God envisions is the group of unity.

Recreation is to resemble God's heart. 
From the principle, we, the descendants of fallen human ancestors today, are like the children of an adulterer before God. No matter how capable someone may be, they cannot be recognized before God. 
We were born with the blood of enemies. Moreover, we were born with the blood of those who deviate from the heavenly principles and those who are traitors. Such people are endlessly shameful regarding God's nation and God's world. 
A group that cannot have hope goes to hell. How long can you claim such a self? Even those who exist in this world, and the nations, are all pitiful. 
Those who walk the path of righteousness must walk alone. In order to be organized, one must organize from the body to the emotional and sensory worlds. 
One must realize that they are less than the dust of all things. 
We must not just rebuild; we must recreate. The responsibility of God is 95 percent, and the responsibility of humans is 5 percent, and together we must build anew. 

Let us say, "Let us go live in our house," meaning "Let us go live in God's house." To do this, we must resemble God. If there is someone who resembles God completely, God will be unable to contain His joy and will say, "You are all my love." 
Today’s youth continually deny the established generation. However, we cannot deny this without resolving it. The Unification Church has appeared to resolve this. We assert that we must resemble those who do not want to resemble. We must resemble everything. One must resemble the king of that nation, and the loyal subjects must resemble each other inside and out. 
We must resemble God. The closest thing to God is the heart. No matter how dark it is, or where one sleeps, the heart is always awake. The day the heart is completely conquered, the body cannot move. 
Without having a relative ideology, one cannot go before God. This is a relationship where the heart and body become one centered on God, and where man and woman become one. 
It is not about believing in Jesus to go to heaven, but one must find the bride to go to heaven by believing in Jesus. 
We must resemble God's heart (vertical) and understand God's circumstances (horizontal) to fulfill God's wishes. And we must know the God of the past, the God of the present, and the God of the future. 
The relationship that strives to resemble the most is that of parent and child. Therefore, there must be both a father and a son.
To become a child of God, one must resemble God's heart. God's heart is 
planted in the world. Therefore, we must love the people of the world. If you cannot love due to distance, you must love your country, your ethnicity, your family, and your parents. This is because parents represent God, spouses represent Adam and Eve, and children represent all of humanity.

Let us become a better reality.
We must fight. We must fight regardless of any difficulties. Thus, a full-scale advance is necessary.

The motivation for war is male, female, I, and you. It is also the struggle of parents, spouses, and siblings. However, there are no enemies in a parent's heart. Therefore, the essence of God is love. 
When you enter the Unification Church, you must become children, brides and grooms, and parents.

You must have a higher family, better parents, siblings, and spouses than your current family. From this perspective, I believe the Unification Church fundamentally presents a new image.

You must understand how miserable the teacher who is pioneering this path is. You must also understand that God, who leads you on this journey, is even more miserable and pitiful.

As I find this house of hope, where am I headed? Once I understand this meaning, it is better to go to the Unification Church than to go home. If not, it is fake, and otherwise, I must walk this path again.

Even among men, you should be able to shed tears because you miss the teacher. You should long to see him just like the heart of a bride and groom.

Those who do not have a beloved younger sister cannot have such a wife, and those who cannot love their mother cannot love their wife.

When a woman enters, she becomes like a father, husband, or older brother, but in the case of men, they stand in a contradictory position to indemnify the circumstances of their fall. That is why they must restore through women.

Jesus is the older brother, the teacher is the younger brother, Jesus is the spiritual husband, the teacher is the substantial husband, Jesus is the spiritual father, and the teacher is the substantial father's position; therefore, we must inherit this.

True Brothers
<Prayer> Father! Today is September 14th, the second holy day of this month. Father, please mold the children gathered here into the image of true love. We have realized that we are the lords of creation, and that your providence to manifest your holiness, goodness, and righteousness is with humanity. As we reflect on this tremendous fact that must bear fruit through humanity at this time, we realize that while each individual is insignificant, there is a tremendous historical connection tied to this insignificant existence.

Born as children of one parent, becoming members of one family, and serving as members of one society, we thought we were living our lives only to meet the end of life. However, we have come to understand through your words that we ourselves are historical realities with significant value.

Father, the Republic of Korea is a pitiful nation. This people has been violated, chased, and persecuted in Asia. There was never a time when this pitiful nation could boast of its rights as humans before heaven. We have realized that we have the mission to indemnify the historical sorrow behind this people. Therefore, we also understand that by indemnifying this sorrow, we can bring forth the eternal blessing of the Father.

On September 14, 1969, at the former headquarters church.
We have come to know that you are the protagonist of sorrow, Father. We also know that you are the holy one who is the source of blessings for all people. Therefore, we have understood that without you, we cannot possess the authority of final victory and the value of ultimate glory, and we have come to know the true meaning that all things and the great trends of the universe are determined by you, the high and precious center.

Since we have received you as our Father, we know that we cannot simply call you Father with our mouths. We have understood the circumstances and feelings of the Father who bears the historical sorrow alone, and we have come to know what the Father's desire is. We have also realized that there was a sincere desire in the Father's heart to find children whom he wanted to command, and that due to the infinite connection of heart, the Father came forth with a pained heart, unable to suppress his sorrow.

When we think that what you have longed for, desired, and required is ourselves today, we cannot help but lament our own miserable and pitiful selves. When we reflect on how we have neglected and given up this fragile connection of life, we must realize that we cannot face the Father without tears, as he seeks to establish this worthless existence with infinite value.

As we delve into the valley of heart and gaze upon your countenance, we come to know how sad, lonely, and pitiful you have been. When we think of this, we realize that we are insufficient beings who dare not call you Father in this state. In terms of bloodline, we have nothing to present with you, as we are the children of enemies. Yet, through your great love, you have allowed us to possess pure value, and we must truly understand how much the internal heart of the Father, who had to love us more than his own children, has suffered.

Even if we were to make a hundredfold or a thousandfold effort, we have come to know that we cannot become beings worthy before the Father's heart.

Father, what can we offer you in gratitude, as you have compassionately looked upon us? We must truly offer our bodies and hearts in gratitude to the Father who has endured through the rough paths to find ourselves, never forgetting that one day. We must become your children who can feel the heart that cannot help but lament, knowing that we cannot face you without tears.

Human beings do not appear as one form in the flowing historical process only to vanish without value; rather, we live as the fruit that can replace the one thought of God's will, centered on the absolute value that cannot be absent in the relationships of heaven and earth. When we think of this fact, we understand that we are not called by anyone but solely by the Father who created the entire universe. We are happy to serve the Father even if we have nothing.

No matter how unfortunate our circumstances may be, when we are with the Father, we are not pitiful, and even if we are in a lonely place, we are not lonely. We know for certain that when we are in the heart that can unite with the Father, the source of strength, there is nothing we cannot accomplish.

Father, when we realize that we, insufficient as we are, are historical realities, our words and actions must not remain within our individual selves. The path we take must not be a path that merely depicts our own lives. We must become your children who can feel the tremendous historical mission of establishing a representative historical origin before this people and all of humanity. We must raise a new banner for goodness. We must become your sons and daughters called to be offerings before the Father, at the solemn altar.

Father, you have called us to fulfill your desires, yet we have nothing to offer before you. Even so, we wish to present our pure hearts, sincere hearts, and true hearts before you, so please grant us this. We earnestly hope to become children who can connect with you with true hearts.

We have called upon you many times only with our mouths. We have called upon you without knowing your circumstances and feelings. You have always called us with a heart full of sorrow, seriousness, and anguish, but we ask for your forgiveness for not being able to understand your heart and not being able to embody the image of worthy sons and daughters.

We know that you sent Jesus to this earth 2,000 years ago to resolve your grievances. Because among countless humanity, there was no one who could understand your heart and fulfill the filial duty with the title of son, you sent Jesus to this earth to resolve the deep feelings that were bound in your heart, representing humanity and history. He grew up alone in the family of Joseph. He had to urge his daily life to become the victorious prince of heaven with a sorrowful heart, having a story that no one knew. However, when we understand the circumstances that Jesus faced, having to endure in an environment where he could not do so, we realize that he was pitiful, lonely, wronged, and miserable. That is why we come to know that Jesus stood closer to the Father.

Let us realize that we are the ones who must inherit this historical content. We have come to know that we have a greater indemnity mission to fulfill through substance than the mission of Jesus. Even while knowing that we have such a tremendous mission, we earnestly ask for your forgiveness for not having devoted all our sincerity to that mission.

We earnestly hope to become your children who can be faithful in the path of restoration that connects the past, present, and future with the Father.

This morning, bodies that were in all directions have gathered here. Please remember your sons and daughters who have come here with busy steps. Is there any child among those gathered here who has come longing for this dawn with a heart concerned for the Father’s name and purpose? Please bestow a thousandfold and ten thousandfold blessings upon that child. Also, if there are children who have come reluctantly, let them realize their shameful selves before heaven and become those who can draw closer to the Father’s heart with a heart of repentance.

At this time, we earnestly hope that you will remember the countless children kneeling alone in various places in South Korea, appealing to you, and we sincerely ask you to remember your children scattered around the world. They are a lonely group. Even if the wind blows, the snow falls, and times and circumstances change, they are a group determined to live only for you, so please remember them. There are countless obstacles in their path. We know that there are always enemy satans blocking the path of your children who call upon you. We must break through the path that those enemies have blocked. We have come to know that we have the mission, responsibility, and duty to remove this, even mobilizing the spirit world, so please cooperate with those who are working in the spirit world to pave their way and protect them.

Thus, we earnestly hope that the day will come soon when we can serve God with peace and sing praises for having become citizens of heaven.

Are there any of your new children here? Please instill in them a heart that longs for and admires the Father. Guide them to forget themselves and be filled with a heart that longs only for the Father, and let them know that without doing so, we cannot have the glory of resurrection.

We earnestly hope that you will accept this day as holy. If there are children who are struggling before you with tears in lonely places, please embrace them with deep heart and nurture them.

We entrust all that will happen from this time onward to you, so please personally oversee it, and we pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> At this time, I will speak on the topic of True Brothers. 
You who are gathered here are people who are walking a new path. We have not gathered for individual purposes but for the purpose of the whole. Therefore, we must prioritize the family over the individual, the nation over the family, and the world over the nation. Moreover, before the individual can be true, the family must be true, and further, the nation and the world must be true.

The Origin of Truth
Human beings stand on the path of restoration where they cannot become the motive of all blessings as individuals. So what is that motive? It is truth. To achieve a true form, humanity must establish a relationship with God, who is the source of all life and death, fortune and misfortune. Without establishing that relationship, one cannot achieve a true form within the individual. Truth must always be centered on God. Therefore, truth is achieved when there is a decisive foundation that can comprehensively guide and govern humanity. If that foundation is not present, it must be understood that the noun "truth" cannot be established.

The origin of truth is God. Truth is realized because God exists. Therefore, when God departs, truth also departs. In that case, the origin of evil, which is not truth, arises. You must understand this fact.

Truth must exist to bring about true results. In other words, it is because God exists that God's will can be fulfilled. Therefore, it must be understood that nouns such as truth and goodness are not established based on humanity but are established based on God.

From this perspective, truth is not something that humans can think of freely. That is, it is not something that fallen humanity can manage at will; rather, we must understand that truth governs us. Therefore, we must always submit to truth. We must establish truth and comply with it.

In your practical lives or in your conscientious lives, it is undeniable that truth is completely related to heaven. Therefore, there must be a true person who possesses true value. When there is a true person, there must be true brothers, and when there are true brothers, there must be true parents. It is the combination of true parents, brothers, and oneself that forms a true family. When such a true family exists, a true lineage emerges from it, and because of that lineage, a true nation and a true world are established.

The Determination of Truth
From this perspective, when we look at the world where 3 billion people live today, how many can we say are true people who can be completely governed by God and possess the contents of God's eternal motive? We can conclude that there are no true people. This is because the definition of truth is still ambiguous.

Globally today, while democracy and communism claim to be right based on ideology, we cannot definitively clarify whether democracy is true or communism is true in the present. Many advocate for them, but there has not yet been anyone who can clarify this with results. We have not encountered such a person.

From this perspective, we understand that ideologies are still in a processional position.
can be. Therefore, we cannot say that the process itself is true. In other words, a fruit that is ripening cannot be called a perfect fruit. It becomes the true fruit only when it is fully ripe. Only then can a new tree be born from that fruit, centered on the true origin. From this perspective, when we look at truth, the true result based on truth has not yet appeared on earth.

Because a true person has not appeared, the true ideology or principle that heaven desires and that our humanity must pursue has not yet emerged. For this reason, although numerous saints and wise individuals have come and gone throughout history, they have only sought after truth; none have lived as true people. This is why the Bible states that there is no righteous person, not even one. The phrase "not even one" implies a denial of oneself. Therefore, truth is not determined from an independent standpoint but must be determined in relation to God. We must understand that this establishes a foundation on earth.

Until now, a true person has not appeared.
Until now, there has been no person on this earth who can completely unite centered on God. That person must appear. The question is how to establish the true origin of history in a world where billions of fallen descendants of humanity live.

When we pray, we often say, "True God, holy God in heaven," out of habit without understanding its true meaning. However, there has been no true meaning of truth until now. Because it has not existed, the origin that can connect to truth is not found in the historical background of humanity but exists in a realm that transcends it. It must start from there. In other words, the origin must be sought from a position that transcends the environment; thus, religion does not center on people and their beliefs. Of course, there are those who establish a standard of faith centered on a religious leader. However, there are also those who transcend that position and pursue truth with God as the intermediary. From this perspective, we can clearly see that there has been no origin of truth in the lives of countless humans who have gone through the historical process or in contemporary society.

In a place connected by humans themselves, it is impossible to establish the origin of truth. Truth must be an absolute standard. Therefore, the issue of God or the Absolute must inevitably arise here. Why is that? Because there has been no true person on earth until now. Because there has been none, a person living with the aim of truth cannot be a motive for truth itself. That motive must be God. At the crucial turning point in the history of religion or humanity, God must appear. The Absolute becomes necessary.

The goal that philosophy pursues, whether through truth or by delving into the origin of existence, must involve the issue of God, the transcendent, and the Absolute. Why is that? Because without establishing a relationship with the Absolute, the origin of all knowledge or the value of existence cannot be resolved. Therefore, when humans are in serious situations, they must establish this relationship and seek resolution through truth.

We cannot deny this fact. Therefore, the origin of truth cannot be established solely by humans; it must involve God, the Absolute, or the Divine. Any religion that claims truth cannot be thought of apart from God. Likewise, any moral or ethical principle that claims truth cannot deny God. This is why Confucius said, "The one who follows heaven will prosper, and the one who goes against heaven will perish." This statement centers on heaven. Heaven must be involved. We must understand that the origin of prosperity and decline is not found in humans themselves but is determined by heaven. In light of this fact, the question arises whether there are true people among humanity living on this earth, as truth cannot exist without the origin that can motivate heaven.

Where can truth reside?
So where can truth reside? Where will it be positioned within humanity? Of course, heaven will be the origin that seeks to establish the place of truth on earth. This is God's desire. Thus, the question becomes where it will reside within humanity. It will not reside in our surroundings, nor in our bodies, but in our hearts. This is why Jesus said, "The kingdom of heaven is within you." The true nation, the kingdom of heaven, resides in the heart. It is situated in a deep valley without any selfish desires.

If we analyze the foundation of our hearts, it consists of intellect, emotion, and will. Among these, where will it reside? When we ask what is fundamental among intellect, emotion, and will, it is emotion. If you have something most precious to you, where would you want to keep it? You would want to keep it in a place only you know. That place is where no one can touch or interfere, a place you can manage absolutely. Where would that be? It is deep within the heart. You would bury it deep in your heart, in a place where you can feel secure. In this sense, the place where truth can reside is the deep part of one's own heart.

Emotion cannot exist alone. It is relative. It must be based on a relative concept. No matter how good a couple may be, if they have no children, they feel lonely. When they are young, they may not realize it, but as they grow older, they feel empty and lonely when they are just with each other. It is more fitting for them to have a child who can serve them. So even while taking the train, you should think, "Yes, I am going well. Today will be the best moment where I can record a precious page in my life." You must be able to say, "Thank you, God." Even in the most difficult and challenging place in the world, you must boldly declare, "I am the number one citizen." To love God, you must be greedy. 

When you go to the local area and think, "The Unification Church's Teacher Moon taught the Principle, and through the Principle, we have become like this!" (laughter) the teacher knows all of this. However, when you come back, you must do that work again. The restoration course has taken 6,000 years until now. 

Based on this principle, the teacher has come this far. There are also Elder Park's group, but has what the Unification Church done until now succeeded or failed? Unification Church members must go to a place where they suffer more than when they were pioneering in Elder Park's evangelistic center. With the faith they had in Elder Park's denomination, they cannot go to heaven. From the perspective of the spirit world, they have not fulfilled their responsibilities. Christian pastors and elders have all failed in their responsibilities. You must restore them in the future. You must go to restore them. This is like a war. Since it is a fierce war, what happens if you win? A love connection that God cannot help but love will be established. There, the sons and daughters of heaven will be determined. The sons and daughters of heaven are not determined on the floor of the headquarters in Seoul, but in a lonely place where neither the teacher nor anyone else is present, they are determined alone.

When humans fell, it was not done under God's membership but was done with Satan as the subject, so Satan must be subdued. 

"Satan! Because I became like this in partnership with you, I will subdue you and return." This must be said. Therefore, unless you receive the certificate of subjugating Satan, you cannot receive God's love. Jesus also won in the three great tests. Without receiving Satan's sign of victory historically, you cannot go to heaven.

The only place that teaches that to go to heaven, you must receive Satan's certificate is the Unification Church. It is qualitatively different from established churches. They explain this without even knowing it for sure.

"Oh, that Teacher Moon of the Unification Church says that to go to heaven, you must receive Satan's certificate, so isn't that Satan?" Did the teacher teach that? They love to promote this. However, we are not to be shaken by such promotions. We must receive Satan's sign by any means necessary. When Jesus was tested by Satan and won, at that moment, Satan shed tears and acknowledged, "You and I are forever different." If one does not acknowledge that, their head will roll off. Do you understand? If you oppose that, your head will be on the line.

The Unification Church must restore all nations 

In the path that the Unification Church is taking, the teacher is carrying the personal cross. The teacher has also carried the cross of the family. You do not know this content. To understand this, you must know the Principle in detail and pray for more than ten years, even if you cannot pray. If parents do not speak of their hardships, children will not know. There are stories that parents cannot tell. Centered around this teacher's family, the blessed families of the Unification Church have the mission to restore all nations on this earth. This is how it continues to grow.

In the past, many people said, "The teachings of the Unification Church are good, but I don't like the Unification Church people. Teacher Moon of the Unification Church is good, but I don't like the president of the Unification Church." I have heard all sorts of comments. If the Unification Church fails, Satan would be pleased, right? However, we must not become Unification Church members that Satan likes. Satan is making things happen so that we can complain. However, within that, true sons and daughters can emerge. They must not all be the same. In that sense, the teacher thinks positively of them.

So, which group is better among those who say the teachings of the Unification Church are good but do not come out because they do not see anything special about the Unification Church and those who come out? The ones who come out are better. Whether they like it or not, they are fighting for the purpose, so the ones who come out are better. When the teacher advances, even if you are at the very back, you must follow. Just following will bring benefits. If in a great battle, all those who participated receive rewards, these will be the first to jump out. (laughter) That is why such things are happening in our church.

From a flat perspective, the established church is in the position of Cain, and our Unification Church is in the position of Abel. Also, within our Unification Church, there are Cain and Abel. In other words, the one who came in first is Abel. However, if one is not careful, it can be reversed. When the firstborn sons and daughters fail to take responsibility, what does God do? He raises a substitute and works through them. Therefore, even within the Unification Church, if the one who came out first makes a mistake, they become Cain, and the one who comes out later becomes Abel.

To restore, Cain must meet Abel, and Abel must meet Cain. 

In the course of restoration, it is structured as the first seven years and the latter seven years.
Yes. Those who joined the Unification Church between 1960 and 1967 correspond to the overall 7-year period. During this time, if you do well, you become the victorious prince; if you do not, you become Cain. What is Cain? He is on the side of Satan. Likewise, within the Unification Church, there are those on the side of Satan and those on the side of Abel. This is why the teacher has treated you this way until now, and even now, after the 7 years have ended, he is expelling even older people. This must be understood clearly.

Why are they being expelled? Because if left alone, you will die. You absolutely cannot survive. Therefore, you must go out to the second front and take responsibility to fight again. Thus, I intend to expel all those who have been here for more than three years. This is because there are people who fall within the second 7-year period. If they become Cain due to their mistakes, they will not even be able to secure their own foothold. No matter how much you pray and struggle, it will not work. The grace of the past will not come back. To return to that state, you must go back. To go back, you must pioneer again. You must restore the path of the pioneer that you have lost. You must move towards the era of individual restoration and family restoration. It may be harder than before, but the content is the same.

You, who are in the second mission period, must not be exhausted. Those who are exhausted cannot be fully responsible for their teacher. You must take responsibility and go on your own. You cannot avoid this path; you must take responsibility and go. When you go to the local areas, even if you want to come to the headquarters church, it is difficult to do so. You will suffer there while longing for the headquarters church. Even when you eat, you sigh and pray. However, if you establish a standard above yourself and connect with someone of a higher standard, that is when the fire of heart ignites. In other words, if Cain does not meet Abel, he cannot restore.

What have you originally lost? You lost the root while trying to fulfill the responsibility to complete the standard of restoration centered on Cain and Abel, that is, to subjugate Satan and be grafted in as children of God. To restore this, you must return to that place. Otherwise, you cannot be grafted in. In other words, you must establish the standard of Cain and Abel to resurrect.

So how do you graft? If you meet a true brother who can graft you, do you die or live? You live without dying. According to principle, the firstborn is the one who will inherit God's lineage. Satan knows this as well. However, that firstborn has become a child of the satanic world. Therefore, God has taken the second son to inherit the firstborn's lineage, but in reality, the firstborn should inherit the lineage. It is reversed. From that perspective, the person Satan loves the most is the only son.

When you engage in evangelism in a certain neighborhood, the first ones to oppose you will be the grandfathers. When they come out believing in the Unification Church, the grandfathers are the first to oppose. These grandfathers come with their pipes, walking in the typical way of the gentry, saying, "Who are these people coming here?" and opposing. Next, people like fathers will oppose. Then, brothers will oppose. You must face opposition from three generations. You cannot avoid opposition. Looking at the history of the fall, the grandfather is like Adam but on the side of Satan. The father is Satan who opposed Jesus. And there must be Cain. Therefore, you must subjugate the Cain grandfather, Cain father, and Cain brother.

This is why, looking at the history of restoration, in the past, every era was a grandfather era. Moses and Noah were in the position of grandfathers. It came down to a younger era in the time of Jesus. Centered around Christianity, it enters the thirties and forties. So what era is the Unification Church today? It is the Cain and Abel era, the young era before marriage. Thus, what has passed through three generations centered on the three eras will now emerge laterally. It will unfold in a plane where it is attacked from the grandfather to the Cain brother.

Knowing this, if there is a grandfather opposing you, you should be glad, saying, "Ah, the grandfather has appeared." If he does not appear, you should make an effort to have him appear. If three such grandfathers appear and oppose, God can find one person. This is an official history. If those who oppose do so vigorously, one person will inevitably be found without you even knowing it. Why is that? Because it is the principle of the son-in-law's expectation. The son-in-law's expectation is heaven. Therefore, if three people oppose, one person can be found. That is how the principle works. Then who usually opposes? It is the men. Women do not tend to oppose. Do grandmothers tremble and oppose? Rather, they worry and say they feel sorry for you and that you are suffering. Also, aunts usually worry thinking about their own children.

To resurrect the Cain of the three brothers, you must become the victorious Abel. The Unification Church has been evangelizing until now with many young people. In other words, from the perspective of the Unification Church itself, it is the era of resurrecting the three generations. Originally, it is not about mobilizing those who have gotten married. It is not about gathering the ragged remnants who have gotten married. Young people must take the lead. You must place pure young women in front to resurrect the three generations.

What standard does heaven want for resurrection? Those who have gotten married and are wearing ragged clothes find it hard to become pure resurrected beings. Heaven desires the resurrection of pure young women. Jesus would also desire such a resurrection. When these young people go out to evangelize, men tend to oppose more. This is because men are archangels.

So why must we focus on these three people? Because without doing so, a revolution cannot be achieved. That is why Jesus also faced three major temptations from Satan. Through the three major temptations, he was restoring first the individual, then the family, and then the world. This represents the three eras of heaven. The history of restoration goes through these representative forms to restore everything.

Where should you align these standards? Should you align them in your own room, or should you go deep into the mountains and enter the lair of Satan? Where should you go? "Into the mountain valley." That is why you are told to go to the local areas. Therefore, the teacher intends to expel the older people in the headquarters before the three years of the second 7-year course are over. All of you here must also go out to evangelize. And you must make decisions for the church.

The teacher has made every possible effort to repay your hard work up until last year, fulfilling all conditional matters. Centered around this issue, you must fulfill the responsibilities entrusted to you to restore this path again. You must long for the spring days of sewing and reminiscing about the past. Since your hearts have frozen like winter, you must prepare to revive while longing for the spring days. Therefore, the headquarters is operating on the principle of sending out at least one more person. This is to follow the principle of restoration. Do you understand?

Then where is the problem? It is in the grafting. You must graft. That is the resurrection of the brother. Abel's victory over Cain lies in the resurrection of the brother. The sorrow of the fall killed the brother. To restore that, you must resurrect the brother. If you cannot resurrect the brother, you cannot restore. Therefore, just because you came in first and are in the position of Abel, you cannot say to those who came in later, in the position of Cain, "Serve me." Even if you came in first, you are an Abel-like Cain centered on the church. You must continue to evangelize Cain-like people, a hundred, a thousand, or more, and connect with them. Through them, you can create a solid foundation where you can stay in the future. It will be a glory for you. However, there are those who do it reluctantly because the teacher commands it. That should not be the case.

You must greet the day of joy centered around yourself. If you felt good seeing the morning sunlight, you should think, "It would be nice to show this sunlight to mom and dad." When you say, "Ah, this is good!" your mother and father will also smile and be happy. In other words, you must motivate your parents to smile by making them happy with your own smile. To do that, you must start with joy and end with joy. You must walk the path of death with joy. Only then will you resurrect with joy.

In the place where life and death are decided, it is a principle that two cannot go together. When Jesus was about to die, he said, "Oh God! After living over thirty years as a disheveled bachelor, how can I die without getting married? That would be so unfair!" If he had succumbed to the people of that time, he would have lost everything. However, Jesus overcame that. He resolved, "Even if I fail in the battlefield, I will not lose the authority of being a son of God." Therefore, he prayed the final prayer in the Garden of Gethsemane, saying, "Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not my will, but yours be done."

He prayed every prayer that a human could offer three times. However, due to the disciples' unfaithfulness, he could not avoid the cross. Seeing the Israelite women following him weeping, Jesus said, "Do not weep for me, but weep for your children." (Luke 23:28) This shows that Jesus understood that much.

What about you? When you reach a place where you could die, do you say, "Oh, please help me! Why do I have to go out to evangelize alone? Why not send two?" You might think, "I'm just a teenager, and if I go out to evangelize, who knows what those rough men will do to me?" It is like sending weak young girls into the midst of wolves. You have heard many bad things about the Unification Church and the teacher from your parents because of this.

However, in that place, two cannot go together. Do life and death begin with two cooperating? When a child is born, do you give birth to two at once? Even if they are twins, they do not come out at the same time. One comes out first, and then the next one comes out. In the place where life and death are decided, it is only alone. You are born alone, and you die alone. No one can participate. No matter how close someone is, they cannot die together. Therefore, instead of saying, "Oh, mom and dad, let's die together," you must leave a will asking them to do everything you wanted to do, even if you die. In other words, you cannot go together in the realm of life and death.

So should you go out to evangelize alone or with someone? You must go alone. Why do you have to go? What should you do? You must run to the enemy, Cain, and graft him to me, Abel. Then you must return after seeing him resurrected in my place. You cannot do otherwise. This is the basic principle of heaven, and there is no other way.

The term "heaven and earth transformation" exists. What does the term "heaven and earth transformation" mean? Is it when a country is turned upside down and the world is turned upside down? Absolutely not. It is when a mother becomes a daughter, and a daughter becomes a mother. (Laughter) There cannot be a greater transformation than that. When parents become children and children become parents, that is the true transformation of heaven and earth. The last becoming first and the first becoming last. When moving forward, you were last, but when you turn around, what happens? (Laughter) This is restoration, that is, the transformation of heaven and earth. The transformation of heaven and earth must happen once. Therefore, the father must become the son, and the son must become the father. Then what happens to the grandfather? He becomes the grandson, and the great-grandfather becomes the great-grandson. From the perspective of the Unification Principle, who is the last grandson in history? It is Adam. Those born in later generations are not the last grandson; they are ancestors. In other words, later generations are not grandsons but ancestors. Do you understand? This is the transformation of heaven and earth.

So what kind of group is the Unification Church? It is a group that is carrying out the movement of the transformation of heaven and earth. Wouldn't the mother and father, and the grandfather oppose? They are fiercely opposing from the world of Satan. To them, we are a band of outlaws. They do not know, but the Unification Principle is structured that way. There is no prestige or face in the world of Satan. The group that goes out with this kind of courage is exactly the Unification Church group. Isn't that amazing? However, the world of Satan is not amazing; it is doomed.

When you go out to evangelize, you must go alone, and when you are to be grafted in, you must be grafted in alone. You must also fight alone against the opposition of Satan. The teacher has always done everything alone to fulfill the will. He has given his all alone. The teacher has no friends. There are many people here, like the association president, but they are not yet brothers. He does everything alone. It feels quite uncomfortable when someone advises the teacher. Listening to advice does not lead to restoration through indemnity. Do you understand? The same goes for you. You cannot restore through indemnity by listening to someone's advice.

If you absolutely obey the command, heaven will work for you. You may rest comfortably, but the teacher of the Unification Church does not rest at night and continues to work. As long as you do not rest, the Unification Church is developing. Even if you gather your belongings and incite a demonstration to kill the teacher, the world will welcome the teacher because he has worked hard. Do you understand? The teacher will not perish. No matter how much the Republic of Korea opposes and how the established churches have opposed for decades, they will never perish.

Although no leaves are visible, the roots are growing deeper and deeper. Then, when spring comes, all the leaves will bloom at once. A big tree grows to its full height and then dies. Isn't that right? However, the Unification Church has deep roots, so no one can uproot it. Not even the teacher can uproot it. Moreover, God cannot uproot it either. The people on the side of Cain are trying to pull us out, but can those guys uproot us? If you dig into the infinitely extending roots, you will find that they extend beyond Adam and Eve to the heart of God, and even God will be brought down. Therefore, the place where the roots are the deepest is the Unification Church. When you hear the principle, you will understand that the place with the deepest roots is the Unification Church. Then, what is resilient? The resilient one is also the Unification Church. The teacher is now nearing 50 years old, but no matter what bet he makes with young people, he will not lose.

No matter what happens, you must evangelize. When the association president says, "You all should evangelize," you might feel, "Oh, that feels bad." You might think, "What does he think he is, to say such things?" and feel bad. Why do you feel bad when you hear the president's words? It is bad because you think it is bad. That should not be the case. On the contrary, when he asks, "Why aren't you evangelizing?" you should feel motivated to do it and think, "Why should I rely on the president?" You should be able to say that. Also, when the teacher says it is a 40-day course, you should think, "I should go out to evangelize." You should be able to say, "I think the way the teacher does it is good." (Laughter) That does not become a sin. Then you can start.

You must absolutely go through the 7-year course. Jesus went through the 3-year course.
has failed. If we had walked the 3-year course and surpassed the 7-year course, we would be moving into our 40s. Wouldn't that be the case? By walking the 3-year course, the first 7-year course must end by the age of 33. However, Jesus could not surpass that. In other words, He could not complete the first 7-year course. He started the first 7-year course and got stuck in the 3-year course. Therefore, He could not achieve the restoration of families.

However, our Unification Church has completed the restoration of families in the 3-year course. From now on, we must carry out a worldwide restoration history. You, who have entered this Unification Church, must have a noble pride. When you stand before the world, you can command freely and live smoothly in the Unification Church. How is it? Is the Unification Church good or bad? "It's good."

However, until we reach a good time, there are challenges. Without the restoration through indemnity, we cannot welcome the good as good. So what do you need to understand? You must absolutely believe and move as one heart when the teacher gives a command centered on the teacher. Then heaven will work. It will definitely work. That is why we can walk the path of restoration today.

To restore through indemnity, we must find and establish true brothers. Right now, the National Assembly of the Republic of Korea is fighting and causing a commotion, but I say, fight well. We are currently conducting a siege operation. We are surrounding the Republic of Korea globally. The 30 million people of this nation must either believe in the Unification Church, die, or run away. (Laughter) It is a fact. The time will come when those who opposed us must either believe in us, not want to believe, die, or run away. We will never perish. No matter how much you look at your palm or read faces, your fate cannot be changed. Since fate is like this, if you do not carry out the restoration through indemnity, you will die. You must pioneer this work with the determination that if you do not do this work, you will die. Through this, you must completely uproot the roots of the satanic world. If that happens, you will be able to claim the glory of heavenly joy.

To do this, true brothers are needed. Without finding true brothers, you cannot serve your parents. You must establish a substantial expectation to welcome the Messiah. In other words, you must find true brothers, who are the substantial expectation to welcome the Lord of the Second Advent. This is the first question to enter heaven.

So how many brothers are needed? Three brothers are needed. You must establish three people who can achieve the expectation centered on yourself. When these three become completely one, I will rise to the position of parents based on that standard of oneness. The blessing determines this position of parents. Therefore, if there are no three children of faith, you cannot receive the blessing. These are the keys to entering heaven. Do you understand? Knowing this, just as Jesus joyfully approached Peter and John, who had rejected him, you must also go to those who have rejected you and completely subjugate them. Even if the Republic of Korea opposes and the established church opposes, you must go.

Then how do we surround and subjugate the established church? The teacher does not lose. Centered on the prestige of denominations and the nation, we have reached a position where we can approach them. Therefore, each of you must find this path. Indemnity must be applied according to the law over a certain period and environment. Otherwise, restoration through indemnity will not happen.

Knowing this, you must establish the position of true brothers. If you do not establish it, nothing will happen. Also, if you are too exhausted to establish it now, that will continue indefinitely. In other words, if you cannot go through the 7-year course, it will be extended again for another 7 or 21 years. However, even if it is extended, you must definitely surpass this.

You must graft in more than three brothers and become their elder. Thus, in the position of Cain, you must allow them to embrace Abel in God's bosom. You must stand in the position of wanting to achieve this. Through that position, you must subjugate Satan and restore your brothers before heaven.

That is the position where God has established Cain, Abel, and Seth. You must stand in the position of the victorious firstborn who has subjugated Satan. Only then can you receive the heavenly achievements and stand before God as their representative, entering the realm of blessing. Thus, you are stepping up on the foundation of heart. Therefore, what is absolutely necessary to enter heaven? "True brothers."

Blessed are the peacemakers, for they shall be called the children of God...

Here, among the Unification Church members, in determining brothers, the one who came first is in the position of Abel and at the same time Cain, and the one who came later is in the position of Cain and at the same time Abel. But can they fight over who will be the firstborn? Would that be good? Such competition is not even competition. When you come to church, there may be people you dislike. There may also be people who hate you. Conversely, there may be people you like. Should there be such people, or should there not? There should be. Thus, there are two groups that are like high mountain ridges and deep valleys, bustling with each other.

Seeing this, Unification Church members have nowhere to put their affection and are throwing themselves into such fights. However, there is only one heavenly prize, and many people want to receive it. They go out together to receive that prize. As the day of receiving that prize approaches, they compete. What do they compete with? They compete with heart. In other words, they compete emotionally.

When I say I love God the most, and I ask God to love me the most, that will fail. However, when I say that the love I have should be received by God and shared with all people, that will not fail. And this must be done discreetly. Therefore, if I say, "I love, but do you not love me?" I will be removed. (Laughter)

The teacher is establishing members based on these principles. The teacher has thought a lot about this. In the spirit world, when showing the competitors, it is amazing. If there is one prize but two people to receive it, there will inevitably be a division between Cain and Abel. You are currently in such a position. However, Unification Church members are indeed good. Unification Church members must value each other.

In that regard, what must you do? You must create true brothers. In other words, you must play the role of grafting. The one who wants to graft a lot is a child of God. However, going around and rubbing off everything that has been grafted is Satan. In other words, being a pillar that grafts is standing in the Abel position, while trying to remove what has been grafted is the fundamental model of Satan. However, among the members, there are those who evaluate others, saying, "This one is like this, and that one is like that." That does not play a supportive role in grafting with God but rather stages a play related to Satan. You must clearly understand this.

In the Gospel of Matthew, it says, "Blessed are the peacemakers, for they shall be called the children of God; blessed are the pure in heart, for they shall see God; blessed are the meek, for they shall inherit the earth." From this perspective, to become the children of God, you must be at peace and united with one another. This is the doctrine of unity.

Here, unity unfolds. When the resurrection of brothers occurs, the tradition of unity is established. For this, brothers must become completely one. They must completely surpass everything that Satan can touch. How much have you established connections to become one in horizontal relationships? Whether you are standing in that position or not will determine whether you can stand close to God in heaven. Therefore, you must find and establish brothers. You must understand that you cannot do without establishing brothers.

<Prayer> Father! As I look at the pitiful humans on this earth who have led a history of resentment on the foundation of grievance until now, I deeply feel that Your merciful hand must be applied here.

Father, we have come to know what true brothers are. Today, we have realized that in this path, the fight between Cain and Abel must transcend not only the front and back relationships but also the up and down, left and right relationships.

In order to resolve this fate, Jesus fought silently, even while being rejected at home, rejected by the nation and people, and chased by the world, to fulfill the Abel-like responsibility for the one heavenly will. He stood at the critical juncture of whether to separate Satan or not, fighting while proclaiming life. I thank You for allowing me to recall this path of Jesus at this time.

Today, I have understood that at the historical final critical juncture of fate, we must separate the front and back, left and right, and up and down. I have also come to know that a true person who can eternally separate heavenly things from earthly things is needed for this important responsibility.

At the same time, I have come to understand that we must become true individuals and establish the connection of true brothers. At this time, I ask that You allow us to analyze the true connection of Cain and Abel within our living sphere and enable us to bear good fruit before You through ourselves. I sincerely hope and wish that this can become our lifelong philosophy of life, allowing us to walk the holy path of serving You.

This morning, please remember Your children scattered across the nation. To those who admire this place from afar, thinking of the teacher and pouring their hearts out before You, I do not wish to be indebted to them, so please repay their grace towards me. I have understood the heart of the Father who blesses those who are devoted and sincere a thousandfold, ten thousandfold, so I ask that You accept my plea for their recommendations and the path of their blessings before You.

I know they will never perish. I see that the fortune of this era will surely intersect with heavenly fortune, and the time of heavenly fortune is increasingly approaching before our eyes. Therefore, I earnestly wish and hope that not a single person will be left behind during this global intersection.

If there are those who are struggling to draw near to You with anxious hearts, please protect them. Hold on to the holy altar so that they may remain within Your grace and especially enable them to attain the glory of victory. I earnestly ask that You make them a group that can be praised before You.

We are those who renew our resolutions daily for that day and become those who prepare internally and externally to show the appearance of victorious warriors before You.

I ask that You govern all things, and I pray in the name of True Parents. Amen. *
